</LuaScriptEntry>
    <LuaScriptEntry Name="Moveset Editor">function UDF1_CEButton1Click(sender)
local count = 0
local char = readInteger("[player1]+168")
local charsettt = 0
local character = 'Character - '
local movnum = readQword("[[player1]+3548+C0]+238")
local movename = 'Move_'
local movename3 = 'Moves -'
local movename2 = '.)  '
local movename1 = 'ID '
local clear = '      -- N/A MOVES -- '
local listcount = UDF1_CEListBox1.Items.Count

if listcount &lt; 1 then
while count &lt; movnum+1 do
  UDF1_CEListBox1.Items.Add(movename1..tostring(char)..movename2..movename..tostring(count))
  count = count + 1
  listcount = listcount + 1
 end
 charsettt = char
else
if charsettt ~= char then
 UDF1_CEListBox1.Items.Text = ""
 UDF1_CELabel2.Caption = ""
 count = 0
 listcount = 0
end
end
UDF1_CELabel2.Caption = movnum
end

function UDF1_CEButton4Click(sender)
local moveidd = readInteger("[player1]+548")
local movnum = readQword("[[player1]+3548+C0]+238")

if moveidd &lt;= movnum+1 then
  playemoveid = getProperty(UDF1_CEEdit1,"Text") -- set vaule of move id
  setProperty(UDF1_CEEdit1,"Text", moveidd)
  UDF1_CEListBox1.ItemIndex = getProperty(UDF1_CEEdit1,"Text")
  setProperty(UDF1_CEEdit2,"Text", moveidd)
  end
end

function UDF1_CEButton24Click(sender)
writeInteger("Exc1", getProperty(UDF1_CEEdit19,"Text"))
writeInteger("Exc2", getProperty(UDF1_CEEdit20,"Text"))
setProperty(UDF1_CEEdit21,"Text",readInteger("Exc1")-readInteger("Exc2"))
end

function UDF1_CEButton2Click(sender)
P1PLAYID = UDF1_CEListBox1.ItemIndex
  setProperty(UDF1_CEEdit1,"Text",P1PLAYID)
  setProperty(UDF1_CEEdit2,"Text",P1PLAYID)
writeInteger("animvalue", getProperty(UDF1_CEEdit2,"Text"))

autoAssemble
[[
aobscanregion(playmoveid,Polaris-Win64-Shipping.exe+18EC2C6,Polaris-Win64-Shipping.exe+18EF71B,89 83 ?? ?? 00 00 E8 ?? ?? ?? ?? 8B 93 ?? ?? 00 00 48 8B CB) // should be unique
alloc(newmem,$1000,playmoveid)
globalalloc(animvalue,4,playmoveid)

label(playcode)
label(return)

newmem:
  cmp [rbx+04],#0
  jne playcode
  push eax
  mov eax,[animvalue]
  cmp eax,0
  pop eax
  jle playcode
  mov eax,[animvalue]
playcode:
  readmem(playmoveid,6)
  jmp return

playmoveid:
  jmp newmem
  nop
return:
registersymbol(playmoveid playcode)
]]
end

function UDF1_CEButton3Click(sender)
autoAssemble
[[
playmoveid:
  readmem(playcode,6)

unregistersymbol(playmoveid)
dealloc(newmem)
]]
end

function UDF1_CEButton40Click(sender)

function UDF1_CEButton41Click(sender)
writeInteger("dnum1", getProperty(UDF1_CEEdit65,"Text"))

end

function UDF1_CEButton8Click(sender)
local count = 0
local char = readInteger("[player2]+168")
local charsettt = 0
local character = 'Character - '
local movnum = readQword("[[player2]+3548+C0]+238")
local movename = 'Move_'
local movename3 = 'Moves -'
local movename2 = '.)  '
local movename1 = 'ID '
local clear = '      -- N/A MOVES -- '
local listcount = UDF1_CEListBox1.Items.Count

if listcount &lt; 1 then
while count &lt; movnum+1 do
  UDF1_CEListBox2.Items.Add(movename1..tostring(char)..movename2..movename..tostring(count))
  count = count + 1
  listcount = listcount + 1
 end
 charsettt = char
else
if charsettt ~= char then
 UDF1_CEListBox2.Items.Text = ""
 UDF1_CELabel4.Caption = ""
 count = 0
 listcount = 0
end
end
UDF1_CELabel4.Caption = movnum
end

function UDF1_CEButton11Click(sender)
local moveidd = readInteger("[player2]+548")
local movnum = readQword("[[player2]+3548+C0]+238")

if moveidd &lt;= movnum+1 then
  playemoveid = getProperty(UDF1_CEEdit3,"Text") -- set vaule of move id
  setProperty(UDF1_CEEdit3,"Text", moveidd)
  UDF1_CEListBox2.ItemIndex = getProperty(UDF1_CEEdit3,"Text")
  setProperty(UDF1_CEEdit4,"Text", moveidd)
  end
end

function UDF1_CEButton9Click(sender)
P1PLAYID = UDF1_CEListBox2.ItemIndex
  setProperty(UDF1_CEEdit3,"Text",P1PLAYID)
  setProperty(UDF1_CEEdit4,"Text",P1PLAYID)
writeInteger("animvalue", getProperty(UDF1_CEEdit4,"Text"))

autoAssemble
[[
aobscanregion(playmoveid,Polaris-Win64-Shipping.exe+18EC2C6,Polaris-Win64-Shipping.exe+18EF71B,89 83 ?? ?? 00 00 E8 ?? ?? ?? ?? 8B 93 ?? ?? 00 00 48 8B CB) // should be unique
alloc(newmem,$1000,playmoveid)
globalalloc(animvalue,4,playmoveid)

label(playcode)
label(return)

newmem:
  cmp [rbx+04],#1
  jne playcode
  push eax
  mov eax,[animvalue]
  cmp eax,0
  pop eax
  jle playcode
  mov eax,[animvalue]
playcode:
  readmem(playmoveid,6)
  jmp return

playmoveid:
  jmp newmem
  nop
return:
registersymbol(playmoveid playcode)
]]
end

function UDF1_CEButton10Click(sender)
autoAssemble
[[
playmoveid:
  readmem(playcode,6)

unregistersymbol(playmoveid)
dealloc(newmem)
]]
end

function UDF1_CEButton12Click(sender)
P1PLAYID = UDF1_CEListBox2.ItemIndex
ADDPLAY = 1
  setProperty(UDF1_CEEdit3,"Text", P1PLAYID-ADDPLAY)
  setProperty(UDF1_CEEdit3,"Text", P1PLAYID-ADDPLAY)
writeInteger("animvalue", getProperty(UDF1_CEEdit3,"Text"))
UDF1_CEListBox2.ItemIndex = getProperty(UDF1_CEEdit3,"Text")

autoAssemble
[[
aobscanregion(playmoveid,Polaris-Win64-Shipping.exe+18EC2C6,Polaris-Win64-Shipping.exe+18EF71B,89 83 ?? ?? 00 00 E8 ?? ?? ?? ?? 8B 93 ?? ?? 00 00 48 8B CB) // should be unique
alloc(newmem,$1000,playmoveid)
globalalloc(animvalue,4,playmoveid)

label(playcode)
label(return)

newmem:
  cmp [rbx+04],#1
  jne playcode
  push eax
  mov eax,[animvalue]
  cmp eax,0
  pop eax
  jle playcode
  mov eax,[animvalue]
playcode:
  readmem(playmoveid,6)
  jmp return

playmoveid:
  jmp newmem
  nop
return:
registersymbol(playmoveid playcode)
]]
end

function UDF1_CEButton43Click(sender)
local count = 0
local char = readInteger("[player1]+168")
local charsettt = 0
local character = 'Character - '
local movnum = 32770
local movename = 'Move_'
local movename3 = 'Moves -'
local movename2 = '.)  '
local movename1 = 'ID '
local clear = '      -- N/A MOVES -- '
local listcount = UDF1_CEListBox1.Items.Count

if listcount &lt; 1 then
while count &lt; movnum+1 do
  UDF1_CEListBox1.Items.Add(movename1..tostring(char)..movename2..movename..tostring(count))
  count = count + 1
  listcount = listcount + 1
 end
 charsettt = char
else
if charsettt ~= char then
 UDF1_CEListBox1.Items.Text = ""
 UDF1_CELabel2.Caption = ""
 count = 0
 listcount = 0
end
end
UDF1_CELabel2.Caption = movnum
end

function UDF2_CEButton13Click(sender)
writeInteger("sidex", -1)
lb=UDF2.CEListBox1 --create a listbox (if added using the formdesigner, use FORMNAME_LISTBOXNAME format)
items=listbox_getItems(lb) --get the Stringlist object that belongs to the listview
strings_add(items," &lt;&lt; Set Both &gt;&gt;")
end

function UDF6_CEButton7Click(sender)

moveline = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit52,"Text")
newanim1 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit53,"Text")
newanim2 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit54,"Text")
newanim3 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit56,"Text")
newanim4 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit57,"Text")
newanim5 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit58,"Text")
newanim6 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit59,"Text")
newanim7 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit60,"Text")
newanim8 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit61,"Text")
newanim9 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit63,"Text")
newanim10 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit64,"Text")
newanim11 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit65,"Text")
newanim12 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit66,"Text")
newanim13 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit67,"Text")
newanim14 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit68,"Text")
newanim15 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit70,"Text")
newanim16 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit71,"Text")
newanim17 = getProperty(UDF6_CEEdit72,"Text")

UDF6_CEListBox2.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox3.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox4.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox5.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox6.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox7.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox8.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox9.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox10.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox11.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox12.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox13.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox14.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox15.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox16.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox17.Items.Delete(moveline)
UDF6_CEListBox18.Items.Delete(moveline)

UDF6_CEListBox2.Items.Insert(moveline,newanim1)
UDF6_CEListBox3.Items.Insert(moveline,newanim2)
UDF6_CEListBox4.Items.Insert(moveline,newanim3)

    <LuaScriptEntry Name="Select Editor">function UDF5_CEListBox1DblClick(sender)
count = UDF5_CEListBox1.Items.Count
for i = 0,count-1 do
 if UDF5_CEListBox1.Selected[i] then
  sltd_item = UDF5_CEListBox1.items[i]
  setProperty(UDF5_CEEdit1,"Text", sltd_item)
  writeInteger("character", UDF5_CEListBox1.ItemIndex)
 else
   --print(list1.Items[i],'not selected')
 end
 end
end

function UDF5_CEListBox2DblClick(sender)

for i = 0,count-1 do
 if UDF5_CEListBox2.Selected[i] then
  sltd_item = UDF5_CEListBox2.items[i]
  setProperty(UDF5_CEEdit2,"Text", sltd_item)
  writeInteger("character", UDF5_CEListBox2.ItemIndex)
 else
   --print(list1.Items[i],'not selected')
 end
 end
end

 if UDF5_CEListBox3.Selected[i] then

function UDF5_CEButton1Click(sender)
if UDF5_CEEdit1.Text == "N/A" then
autoAssemble
[[
INJECT:
  db 42 8B 44 01 10

unregistersymbol(INJECT)
dealloc(newmem)
]]
showMessage'Clear Select!'
end
if UDF5_CEEdit1.Text ~= "N/A" then
autoAssemble
[[
aobscanmodule(INJECT,Polaris-Win64-Shipping.exe,42 8B 44 01 10 C3 CC CC CC CC CC CC 4C) // should be unique
alloc(newmem,$1000,INJECT)


label(code)
label(return)

newmem:
   mov eax,[sides]
   cmp rdx,eax
   jne code
   mov eax,[character]
   mov [rcx+r8+10],eax
   add rax,r8
code:
  mov eax,[rcx+r8+10]
  jmp return

INJECT:
  jmp newmem
return:
registersymbol(INJECT)
]]
showMessage'Character Select!!'
end
end

function UDF5_CEButton3Click(sender)
if UDF5_CEEdit3.Text == "N/A" then
autoAssemble
[[
stageselect:
  db 89 91 98 01 00 00

unregistersymbol(stageselect)
dealloc(newmem)
]]
showMessage'Clear Select!'
end
if UDF5_CEEdit3.Text ~= "N/A" then
autoAssemble
[[
aobscanmodule(stageselect,Polaris-Win64-Shipping.exe,89 91 98 01 00 00 8B) // should be unique
alloc(newmem,$1000,stageselect)

label(code)
label(return)

newmem:
  mov rax,01
  mov eax,[stages]
  mov rdx,eax
  mov rdi,01
code:
  mov [rcx+00000198],edx
  jmp return

stageselect:
  jmp newmem
  nop
return:
registersymbol(stageselect)
]]
showMessage'Stage Select!!'
end
end

    <LuaScriptEntry Name="Save/Load">local sf = os.getenv("USERPROFILE") .. "\\Documents\\";
if sf then
os.execute([[mkdir "]]..sf..[[\Save_Moveset 5.0"]]) -- create folder
end


local pth=sf..[[Save_Moveset 5.0\]] -- or sf.."My Cheat Tables\\"

local s1f = os.getenv("USERPROFILE") .. "\\Documents\\Save_Moveset 5.0\\";
if s1f then
os.execute([[mkdir "]]..s1f.."Animation IDs"..[[\"]]) -- create folder
end

local s1f = os.getenv("USERPROFILE") .. "\\Documents\\Animation IDs\\";
if s1f then
os.execute([[mkdir "]]..s1f.."Animation IDs"..[[\"]]) -- create folder
end


function UDF2_CEButton10Click(sender)
shellExecute(pth)
end

function UDF2_CEButton8Click(sender)
local s1f = os.getenv("USERPROFILE") .. "\\Documents\\Save_Moveset 5.0\\";
if s1f then
os.execute([[mkdir "]]..s1f..UDF2_CEEdit1.Text..[[\"]]) -- create folder

local pth1=s1f..UDF2_CEEdit1.Text..[[/]] -- or sf.."My Cheat Tables\\"


SAVEMOVE= getProperty(UDF2_CEEdit1,"Text")
 UDF2_CEListBox2.items.Add(SAVEMOVE)

local text2=pth1..UDF2_CEEdit1.Text.." (Replace).txt"
if text2 then
local settingsFile = io.open(text2, "w")
    if (settingsFile ~= nil) then
      lb=UDF2.CEListBox1 --create a listbox (if added using the formdesigner, use FORMNAME_LISTBOXNAME format)
      items=listbox_getItems(lb) --get the Stringlist object that belongs to the listview
      strings_add(items," &lt;&lt; Saving Replace Moves ... &gt;&gt;")
      settingsFile:write(UDF1_CEListBox4.Items.Text)
      settingsFile:close()
    end
  end
local text3=pth1..UDF2_CEEdit1.Text.." (ReplaceVaules).txt"
if text3 then
local settingsFile = io.open(text3, "w")
    if (settingsFile ~= nil) then
      settingsFile:write(UDF1_CEListBox5.Items.Text)
      settingsFile:close()
    end
  end
  local text6=pth1..UDF2_CEEdit1.Text.." (HitReaction).txt"
if text6 then
local settingsFile = io.open(text6, "w")

function UDF2_CEButton11Click(sender)
local s1f = os.getenv("USERPROFILE") .. "\\Documents\\Save_Moveset 5.0\\";
if s1f then
os.execute([[mkdir "]]..s1f..UDF2_CEEdit1.Text..[[\"]]) -- create folder

local pth2=s1f..UDF2_CEEdit1.Text..[[/]] -- or sf.."My Cheat Tables\\"

local text52=pth2..UDF2_CEEdit1.Text.." (Replace).txt"
if text52 then
local settingsFile = io.open(text52, "r")
    if (settingsFile ~= nil) then
      lb=UDF2.CEListBox1 --create a listbox (if added using the formdesigner, use FORMNAME_LISTBOXNAME format)
      items=listbox_getItems(lb) --get the Stringlist object that belongs to the listview
      strings_add(items," &lt;&lt; Loading Replace Moves ... &gt;&gt;")
      UDF1_CEListBox4.Items.Text = settingsFile:read("*a"):gsub("\n\r", "")
      settingsFile:close()
    end
  end
local text53=pth2..UDF2_CEEdit1.Text.." (ReplaceVaules).txt"
if text53 then

function UDF2_CEListBox2DblClick(sender)
count = UDF2_CEListBox2.Items.Count
for i = 0,count-1 do
 if UDF2_CEListBox2.Selected[i] then
  sltd_item = UDF2_CEListBox2.items[i]
  setProperty(UDF2_CEEdit1,"Text", sltd_item)
 else
   --print(list1.Items[i],'not selected')
 end
 end
end

function UDF2_CEButton9Click(sender)
local text100=pth..UDF2_CEEdit2.Text.." (Data).txt"
if text100 then
local settingsFile = io.open(text100, "r")
    if (settingsFile ~= nil) then
      UDF2_CEListBox2.Items.Text = settingsFile:read("*a"):gsub("\n\r", "")
      settingsFile:close()
    end
  end
showMessage "Movelist-Updated"
end
</LuaScriptEntry>
  </LuaScript>
</CheatTable>
